msg:It is called a five-star hotel and the best hotel in Gui'an New District. The rooms are really big. There are mountains and lakes around the hotel. The external environment is first-class, and the room decoration is second-class and slightly old, but the service is not up to standard. I stayed there for two nights on 22nd and 23rd. There was no hot water in the whole hotel on the night of the 23rd. It was speechless that there was no hot water until 11 o'clock in the evening. The front desk phone was always busy, but the front desk could be connected in seconds when calling the outside line with a mobile phone. It feels like it should have been a very good existence ten years ago, but ten years have passed, and the hardware is still the same as it was ten years ago, and the software and service have degenerated to the level of a guesthouse. If it is not for business, I will not choose to live here.
